+    <script>
+        // POINT 1: Security Accordion
+        function toggleSecurity(element) {
+            const items = document.querySelectorAll('.security-accordion-item');
+            const isActive = element.classList.contains('active');
+            items.forEach(item => item.classList.remove('active'));
+            if (!isActive) element.classList.add('active');
+        }
+
+        // POINT 3: Tilt Effect JavaScript
+        const handleTilt = (e) => {
+            const tiltCards = document.querySelectorAll('.tilt-card');
+            tiltCards.forEach(card => {
+                const rect = card.getBoundingClientRect();
+                const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
+                const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
+
+                if (x > 0 && x < rect.width && y > 0 && y < rect.height) {
+                    const centerX = rect.width / 2;
+                    const centerY = rect.height / 2;
+                    const rotateX = (centerY - y) / 10;
+                    const rotateY = (x - centerX) / 10;
+                    card.style.transform = `perspective(1000px) rotateX(${rotateX}deg) rotateY(${rotateY}deg) scale3d(1.05, 1.05, 1.05)`;
+                } else {
+                    card.style.transform = `perspective(1000px) rotateX(0deg) rotateY(0deg) scale3d(1, 1, 1)`;
+                }
+            });
+        };
+
+        document.addEventListener('mousemove', handleTilt);
+    </script>
 </body>

+    <script>
+        // L├│gica de Ventajas Desplegables
+        function toggleAdvantage(element) {
+            const items = document.querySelectorAll('.advantage-item');
+            const isActive = element.classList.contains('active');
+
+            // Cerrar todos primero
+            items.forEach(item => item.classList.remove('active'));
+
+            // Si el que clickeamos no estaba activo, lo activamos
+            if (!isActive) {
+                element.classList.add('active');
+            }
+        }
+    </script>

+                                    <option class="text-black">M├ís de 1000</option>

+                            class="w-full py-4 rounded-xl text-black font-bold text-lg mt-4 transition-all hover:scale-[1.02] hover:shadow-[0_0_40px_rgba(0,217,255,0.4)]"
+                            style="background-color: var(--primary); box-shadow: 0 15px 30px rgba(0,217,255,0.3);">
+                            Solicitar evaluaci├│n t├⌐cnica confidencial

+    <!-- SCRIPTS M├üGICOS -->
+    <script>
+        // 1. Iniciar Lucide Icons
+        lucide.createIcons();
+
+        // 2. Animaciones de scroll (Intersection Observer)
+        const observerOptions = {
+            root: null,
+            rootMargin: '0px',
+            threshold: 0.15
+        };
+
+        const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries, observer) => {
+            entries.forEach(entry => {
+                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
+                    entry.target.classList.add('reveal-active');
+                    observer.unobserve(entry.target);
+                }
+            });
+        }, observerOptions);
+
+        document.querySelectorAll('.reveal-up, .reveal-left, .reveal-right, .reveal-scale').forEach((el) => {
+            observer.observe(el);
+        });
+
+        // 3. L├│gica del Selector de Tipograf├¡as Din├ímico
+        const fonts = {
+            pantonThin: { name: 'Panton Thin', family: 'Panton', weight: 100, italic: false },
+            pantonLight: { name: 'Panton Light', family: 'Panton', weight: 300, italic: false },
+            pantonRegular: { name: 'Panton Regular', family: 'Panton', weight: 400, italic: false },
+            pantonSemiBold: { name: 'Panton SemiBold', family: 'Panton', weight: 600, italic: false },
+            pantonBold: { name: 'Panton Bold', family: 'Panton', weight: 700, italic: false },
+            pantonExtraBold: { name: 'Panton ExtraBold', family: 'Panton', weight: 800, italic: false },
+            pantonBlack: { name: 'Panton Black', family: 'Panton', weight: 900, italic: false },
+
+            spaceLight: { name: 'Space Grotesk Light', family: 'Space Grotesk', weight: 300, italic: false },
+            spaceRegular: { name: 'Space Grotesk Regular', family: 'Space Grotesk', weight: 400, italic: false },
+            spaceMedium: { name: 'Space Grotesk Medium', family: 'Space Grotesk', weight: 500, italic: false },
+            spaceSemiBold: { name: 'Space Grotesk SemiBold', family: 'Space Grotesk', weight: 600, italic: false },
+            spaceBold: { name: 'Space Grotesk Bold', family: 'Space Grotesk', weight: 700, italic: false },
+
+            rajdhaniLight: { name: 'Rajdhani Light', family: 'Rajdhani', weight: 300, italic: false },
+            rajdhaniRegular: { name: 'Rajdhani Regular', family: 'Rajdhani', weight: 400, italic: false },
+            rajdhaniMedium: { name: 'Rajdhani Medium', family: 'Rajdhani', weight: 500, italic: false },
+            rajdhaniSemiBold: { name: 'Rajdhani SemiBold', family: 'Rajdhani', weight: 600, italic: false },
+            rajdhaniBold: { name: 'Rajdhani Bold', family: 'Rajdhani', weight: 700, italic: false },
+
+            exoExtraLight: { name: 'Exo 2 ExtraLight', family: 'Exo 2', weight: 200, italic: false },
+            exoLight: { name: 'Exo 2 Light', family: 'Exo 2', weight: 300, italic: false },
+            exoRegular: { name: 'Exo 2 Regular', family: 'Exo 2', weight: 400, italic: false },
+            exoMedium: { name: 'Exo 2 Medium', family: 'Exo 2', weight: 500, italic: false },
+            exoSemiBold: { name: 'Exo 2 SemiBold', family: 'Exo 2', weight: 600, italic: false },
+            exoBold: { name: 'Exo 2 Bold', family: 'Exo 2', weight: 700, italic: false },
+            exoExtraBold: { name: 'Exo 2 ExtraBold', family: 'Exo 2', weight: 800, italic: false },
+            exoBlack: { name: 'Exo 2 Black', family: 'Exo 2', weight: 900, italic: false },
+        };
+
+        let activeFontKey = 'pantonRegular';
+        const fontGrid = document.getElementById('fontGrid');
+
+        function renderFontButtons() {
+            fontGrid.innerHTML = '';
+            for (const [key, fontDef] of Object.entries(fonts)) {
+                const isActive = key === activeFontKey;
+
+                const btn = document.createElement('button');
+                btn.className = `px-3 py-2.5 rounded-md border transition-all text-left ${isActive ? 'border-scheme-primary bg-scheme-primary/20 text-[#00D9FF]' : 'border-white/20 hover:border-scheme-primary/50 text-white/70 hover:text-white'}`;
+                btn.style.fontFamily = `'${fontDef.family}', sans-serif`;
+                btn.style.fontWeight = fontDef.weight;
+                if (isActive) btn.style.boxShadow = '0 0 15px rgba(0, 217, 255, 0.3)';
+
+                btn.innerHTML = `<span class="text-xs">${fontDef.name}</span>`;
+
+                btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
+                    activeFontKey = key;
+                    applyFont(key);
+                    renderFontButtons(); // Re-render for active state
+                });
+
+                fontGrid.appendChild(btn);
+            }
+        }
+
+        function applyFont(key) {
+            const font = fonts[key];
+            const fontFamily = `'${font.family}', sans-serif`;
+            const fontWeight = font.weight;
+            const fontStyle = font.italic ? 'italic' : 'normal';
+
+            // Actualizar el body por defecto
+            document.body.style.fontFamily = fontFamily;
+            document.body.style.fontWeight = fontWeight;
+            document.body.style.fontStyle = fontStyle;
+
+            // Inyectar estilos globales para forzar en t├¡tulos y elementos con clases de peso
+            let dynamicStyle = document.getElementById('dynamic-font-overrides');
+            if (!dynamicStyle) {
+                dynamicStyle = document.createElement('style');
+                dynamicStyle.id = 'dynamic-font-overrides';
+                document.head.appendChild(dynamicStyle);
+            }
+
+            dynamicStyle.innerHTML = `
+                h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6, 
+                .font-light, .font-normal, .font-medium, .font-semibold, .font-bold, .font-black,
+                button, .btn-primary { 
+                    font-family: ${fontFamily} !important;
+                    font-weight: ${fontWeight} !important;
+                    font-style: ${fontStyle} !important;
+                }
+            `;
+        }
+
+        // Initialize
+        applyFont(activeFontKey);
+        renderFontButtons();
+
+        // 4. L├│gica de Colapso del Men├║
+        const fontToggle = document.getElementById('fontMenuToggle');
+        const fontPanel = document.getElementById('fontMenuPanel');
+        const fontChevron = document.getElementById('fontChevron');
+
+        fontToggle.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+            e.stopPropagation();
+            const isHidden = fontPanel.classList.contains('hidden');
+            if (isHidden) {
+                fontPanel.classList.remove('hidden');
+                fontChevron.style.transform = 'rotate(180deg)';
+                fontToggle.style.borderColor = 'var(--primary)';
+            } else {
+                fontPanel.classList.add('hidden');
+                fontChevron.style.transform = 'rotate(0deg)';
+                fontToggle.style.borderColor = 'rgba(0,217,255,0.5)';
+            }
+        });
+
+        // Cerrar al hacer clic fuera
+        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
+            if (!fontPanel.contains(e.target) && !fontToggle.contains(e.target)) {
+                fontPanel.classList.add('hidden');
+                fontChevron.style.transform = 'rotate(0deg)';
+                fontToggle.style.borderColor = 'rgba(0,217,255,0.5)';
+            }
+        });
+
+        // 5. Part├¡culas del Puma (Running Effect)
+        function initPumaParticles() {
+            const canvas = document.getElementById('pumaParticles');
+            if (!canvas) return;
+            const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
+            let particles = [];
+            let w, h;
+
+            function resize() {
+                const parent = canvas.parentElement;
+                w = canvas.width = parent.offsetWidth;
+                h = canvas.height = parent.offsetHeight;
+            }
+
+            class Particle {
+                constructor() {
+                    this.reset();
+                }
+                reset() {
+                    // Aparecen mayormente por la derecha para simular avance
+                    this.x = Math.random() * w;
+                    this.y = Math.random() * h;
+                    // Velocidad horizontal alta hacia la izquierda (simula que el puma va a la derecha)
+                    this.vx = -(Math.random() * 5 + 2);
+                    this.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5;
+                    this.size = Math.random() * 2 + 0.5;
+                    // Colores morados y cian
+                    const isPurple = Math.random() > 0.5;
+                    this.color = isPurple ? '168, 85, 247' : '0, 217, 255';
+                    this.alpha = Math.random() * 0.6 + 0.2;
+                }
+                update() {
+                    this.x += this.vx;
+                    this.y += this.vy;
+                    if (this.x < -10) this.x = w + 10;
+                    if (this.y < 0 || this.y > h) this.reset();
+                }
+                draw() {
+                    ctx.beginPath();
+                    // Dibujar una peque├▒a estela (streak) para dinamismo
+                    ctx.moveTo(this.x, this.y);
+                    ctx.lineTo(this.x - this.vx * 2, this.y);
+                    ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(${this.color}, ${this.alpha})`;
+                    ctx.lineWidth = this.size;
+                    ctx.stroke();
+
+                    ctx.beginPath();
+                    ctx.arc(this.x, this.y, this.size, 0, Math.PI * 2);
+                    ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(${this.color}, ${this.alpha})`;
+                    ctx.fill();
+                }
+            }
+
+            function init() {
+                resize();
+                particles = [];
+                for (let i = 0; i < 150; i++) particles.push(new Particle());
+            }
+
+            function animate() {
+                ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);
+                particles.forEach(p => {
+                    p.update();
+                    p.draw();
+                });
+                requestAnimationFrame(animate);
+            }
+
+            window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
+            init();
+            animate();
+        }
+
+        initPumaParticles();
+    </script>
+</body>
+
+</html>
